[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA Jazzer fuzzing run triggered a `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh` indicating a potential [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremote code execution vulnerability. The issue arises from unrestricted class or [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mobject creation during deserialization of external data. The stack trace shows the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproblem surfaced while parsing an RTF document with embedded objects, ultimately [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoking `java.io.ObjectInputStream.readObject` on attacker-controlled input.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  During fuzz testing of an RTF parser, the fuzzer encountered a [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh` exception. The message [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreports “Remote Code Execution” due to “Unrestricted class/object creation based on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternally controlled data.”  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type:  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Insecure deserialization leading to remote code execution, as flagged by Jazzer’s[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msecurity checks.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations and Findings:  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The exception is thrown from `jaz.Zer.reportFinding`, called by [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jaz.Zer.readObject`, indicating that the fuzzer detected an unsafe deserialization[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The Java built-in `ObjectInputStream.readObject` API is used to parse [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserialized data embedded within an RTF document.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The parsing chain runs through Apache Tika’s RTF modules:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.tika.parser.microsoft.rtf.RTFEmbObjHandler.handleCompletedObject`  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `org.apache.tika.parser.microsoft.rtf.TextExtractor.processGroupEnd`  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `org.apache.tika.parser.microsoft.rtf.RTFParser.parseInline` and `parse`  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. The user’s fuzzing harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`com.example.RTFParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis merely the entry point and not the root cause; it supplies potentially malicious[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRTF inputs to the parser.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas to Investigate:  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • All deserialization logic in Apache Tika’s RTF parser, especially in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RTFEmbObjHandler` and related handlers.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The use of `java.io.ObjectInputStream` or similar APIs for reading embedded [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mserialized objects.  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Any configuration or utility methods that govern class resolution or filtering [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring deserialization.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The integration points between the fuzzing harness and the parser to understand[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow untrusted data flows into the deserialization routines.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzer flagged a high-severity remote code execution issue in Apache       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Tika’s RTF parser. The vulnerability arises from unrestricted Java deserialization  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         of embedded object data in `RTFEmbObjHandler`. To mitigate, a patch was proposed    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         that removes the `[1;35mObjectInputStream.readObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m` call and instead logs a           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `TikaException` via `[1;35membeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m`, skipping further   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         processing of Java‐embedded data. After applying the patch, the module fails to     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         compile with a cascade of “illegal start of type,” “identifier expected,” and       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         “invalid method declaration” errors in `RTFEmbObjHandler.java`.                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. Initial Issue                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer security fuzzer reported `FuzzerSecurityIssueHigh: Remote Code        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Execution` in the RTF parser.                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Stack trace pinpoints `[1;35mRTFEmbObjHandler.handleCompletedObject[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m` in the     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA` branch, where untrusted byte streams are fed into `new     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mObjectInputStream[0m[1m([0m[33m...[0m[1m)[0m[1;35m.readObject[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m`.                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This allows an attacker to instantiate arbitrary classes present on the        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         classpath, leading to potential RCE.                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. Important Observations                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerable code lives inside an `else if [1m([0mstate ==                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA[1m)[0m` block in `RTFEmbObjHandler.java`.                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A `try` block deserializes the byte array, extracts class name into metadata,  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         and converts the object to a plain-text fallback.                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A catch for `ClassNotFoundException` wraps missing-class errors in a           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `TikaException`.                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. Patch Attempt                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The patch removes the entire deserialization `try`[35m/[0m`catch` and its logic.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - In its place it inserts:                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [35m/[0m[35m/[0m Disable embedded Java object deserialization for security                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [1;35membeddedDocumentUtil.recordException[0m[1m([0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  new [1;35mTikaException[0m[1m([0m[32m"Embedded Java object deserialization is disabled"[0m[1m)[0m,     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  metadata[1m)[0m;                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [35m/[0m[35m/[0m Skip further processing of this embedded data                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The intent is to disable Java object data handling and flag the issue without  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         executing dangerous code.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. Compilation Result                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - After patching, `mvn compile` in the Microsoft parser module fails with ~[1;36m24[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         errors.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Errors such as “illegal start of type,” “[1m<[0m[1;95midentifier[0m[39m> expected,” and “invalid [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod declaration; return type required” all refer to lines in [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`RTFEmbObjHandler.java` around the patched region.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The mass of “class, interface, enum, or record expected” suggests a mismatched[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrace or misplaced code fragment that breaks the class’s structure.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Further Investigation Areas  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Verify the brace structure around the `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstate == EMB_STATE.JAVA_OBJDATA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m  [2m                [0m
